1. There are not many varieties of hotel breakfast, and the range of choices is relatively small.
2. The design of the room is unreasonable, and the sliding door of the bathing room is very cramped, and it is easy to pinch your hands if you are not careful. Then there are 2 washbasins in the bathroom and the shower room, and it is not convenient to wash. All bath towels are behind the bathtub, and it is inconvenient to get them out of the rain.
3. I hope that the bath products can be replaced with better well-known brands.
4. The bed is too soft to sleep comfortably
The service level in other aspects is still good, and they specially brought us bathrobes, slippers, and toiletries for the children.

The toothbrush and slippers are the worst disposable products. There is no comfort at all. They are almost the same as a four-star hotel like Crystal Orange. .
There is nothing in the small refrigerator in the room. Except for instant coffee and tea, there is no other snacks and drinks in the entire minibar. It is worse than some four-star hotels. The air-conditioning panel shows heat when I enter the room. I called and the customer service told me that the air-conditioning cannot be used in a single room. Adjust the temperature? ? ? ? That is to say, all guests cannot have their own temperature preferences and can only accept unified arrangements.
I was hungry in the early morning and wanted to order something to eat. The customer service said that room service was not available 24 hours a day. It was really the first time I encountered such a "five-star" hotel.
But maybe this store doesn't care about other people's evaluations. After all, the hardware and services are at this level. At first glance, it seems that it is not pursuing a true five-star level. It just wants to make money by using the Hilton brand.
